***gezind.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gezind.html>gezind</a> (13389)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gezind.html>gezind</a></strong> (<i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>inclined, of a certain disposition
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:goden.html>goden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vandaag.html>vandaag</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gunstig.html>gunstig</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gezind.html>gezind</a></b>.</i>
<dl><dd>The <a href = vnd.unilang:gods.html>gods</a> are favourably inclined today.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>This word <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> rarely used alone. It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> usually preceded by an adverb to specify what <a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kind</a> of disposition.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gesontheid</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:gesundheit.html>Gesundheit</a></i>.

***gezwind.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gezwind.html>gezwind</a> (47322)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">geschwind</i> (late 16th century), a prefixed variant of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">swind</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">*swind</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*swinþaz</i>. Thence also <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">swith</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gothic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gothic language">Gothic</a></span> <i class="Goth mention" lang="got">𐍃𐍅𐌹𐌽𐌸𐍃</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="got-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">swinþs</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gezwind.html>gezwind</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gezwind.html>gezwinder</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">gezwindst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> rapid, brisk
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:snel.html>snel</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">rap</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vlug.html>vlug</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

***gids.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gids.html>gids</a> (4312)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Probably borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Romani_language" class="extiw" title="w:Romani language">Romani</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="rom">gaʒo</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="rom">gadjo</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">Non-Romani; farmer</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, with influence from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">guide</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gids.html>gids</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gidsen.html>gidsen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gidsje.html>gidsje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">guide</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">person guiding others</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dan.html>Dan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kan.html>kan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gids.html>gids</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ons.html>ons</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stad.html>stad</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:laten.html>laten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zien.html>zien</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Then the <b>guide</b> can let us see the town.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vergeet.html>Vergeet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gids.html>gids</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Don'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> forget the <b>guide</b>.</span></div></dd></dl></li>

***gieren.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gieren.html>gieren</a> (12461)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ghieren</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">gīren</i>, whence <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:gieren.html>gieren</a></i>. Eventually onomatopoeic.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gieren.html>gieren</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to <a href = vnd.unilang:screech.html>screech</a>, to shriek</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to roar with laughter, to laugh loudly</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gier.html>gier</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">liquid manure</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">agriculture<span class="ib-comma">,</span> intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fertilise <a href = vnd.unilang:land.html>land</a> with slurry, to spread liquid manure</li></ol>

***gif.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gif.html>gif</a> (3771)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gift</i>, earlier also <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gicht</i>. From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*gift</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*giftiz</i>. The word <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">gift</i> derives from the same source and the <a href = vnd.unilang:words.html>words</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> not formally distinguished until early modern Dutch.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<ol><li>poison, venom, toxin</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gifmenger.html>gifmenger</a> (117259)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gif.html>gif</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">poison</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">menger</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mixer, one who mixes</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gifmenger.html>gifmenger</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gifmengers.html>gifmengers</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>One who mixes poison into food or drinks, a <span class="Latn" lang="en">poisoner</span>.
<ul><li><b>1723</b> May 18, <a href = vnd.unilang:jacob.html>Jacob</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:campo.html>Campo</a> Weyerman, <i>Den Amsterdamschen <a href = vnd.unilang:hermes.html>Hermes</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:vol.html>Vol</a>. 2, No. 34, page 267.

<ol><li>A fang, a hollow type of tooth which venomous <a href = vnd.unilang:creatures.html>creatures</a> use to inject poison in a prey or enemy.</li></ol>

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">SI</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> 10<sup>9</sup>, one billion (1,000,000,000) <a href = vnd.unilang:bytes.html>bytes</a>. SI symbol: GB
<ul><li><b>1981</b>, IBM, <i><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20121004012720/http://bitsavers.informatik.uni-stuttgart.de/pdf/ibm/dasd/GA26-1664-1_3380_IBM_3380_Direct_Access_Storage_Description_and_Users_Guide_Dec81.pdf">IBM 3380 Direct Access Storage Description and User's Guide</a></i>, page 1
<dl><dd>The IBM 3380 Direct Access Storage <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a disk storage device with a storage capacity of 2.5 <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gigabytes.html>gigabytes</a></b> (billion <a href = vnd.unilang:bytes.html>bytes</a>) per unit, an increase of almost four times the capacity of the IBM 3350 Direct Access Storage.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">computing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a gibibyte or 1024<sup>3</sup> (1,073,741,824) <a href = vnd.unilang:bytes.html>bytes</a>.</li></ol>

***gij.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gij.html>gij</a> (2725)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gī</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ghi</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">gī</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*jīz</i>, Northwest Germanic variant of <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*jūz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*yū́</i>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jij.html>jij</a></i>.
</p><p>Compare also <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">ji</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">jie</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">ye</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">ihr</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gij.html>gij</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dialectal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> you
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:motten.html>Motte</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gij.html>gij</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:nog.html>nog</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> pilske?</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Do <b>you</b> want another <a href = vnd.unilang:beer.html>beer</a>?.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic<span class="ib-comma">,</span> literary<span class="ib-comma">,</span> religious</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> thou
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:gij.html>Gij</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:zult.html>zult</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:doden.html>doden</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>Thou</b> shalt not kill.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>In most of the Netherlands, the personal pronoun <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gij.html>gij</a></i> and its variants are now mainly used in religious context and are considered archaic. In Flanders and the southern Netherlands, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gij.html>gij</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> still commonly used as the second-person singular in colloquial language; in formal language it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not used unless the referred second person <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the "<a href = vnd.unilang:god.html>god</a>" or the "king".</li></ul>
<ul><li>The <a href = vnd.unilang:best.html>best</a> translation when used in archaic contexts would be <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">thou</i>; when used in Flanders or the southern Netherlands, it would typically be <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">you</i> (singular). Unlike in English, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gij.html>gij</a></i> usually <a href = vnd.unilang:takes.html>takes</a> the same verb form as <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jij.html>jij</a></i> except when there <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> inversion or with some irregular verbs or in the past tense. Compare <i><a href = vnd.unilang:heb.html>heb</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jij.html>jij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dit.html>dit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gedaan.html>gedaan</a>?</i> versus <i><a href = vnd.unilang:hebt.html>hebt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gij.html>gij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dit.html>dit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gedaan.html>gedaan</a>?</i> (have you / hast thou done this?). Also: <i><a href = vnd.unilang:jij.html>jij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zal.html>zal</a></i> versus <i><a href = vnd.unilang:gij.html>gij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zult.html>zult</a></i> (you shall/will / thou shalt/<a href = vnd.unilang:wilt.html>wilt</a>), <i><a href = vnd.unilang:jij.html>jij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bent.html>bent</a></i> versus <i><a href = vnd.unilang:gij.html>gij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijt.html>zijt</a></i> (you are / thou art), <i><a href = vnd.unilang:jij.html>jij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vloog.html>vloog</a></i> versus <i><a href = vnd.unilang:gij.html>gij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vliegen.html>vloogt</a></i> (you flew / thou flewest) etc.</li></ul>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">giseler</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">giselaer</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gisel</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">-aer</i>. The former derives from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*gīsel</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*gīslaz</i>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gilde.html>gilde</a> (7302)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:gilde.html>gilde</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ghilde</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gulde</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:gilda.html>gilda</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*geldaną</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to pay</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gillen.html>gillen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>.

***gin.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gin.html>gin</a> (6477)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Abbreviation of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">geneva</i> or alternatively from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">genever</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">juniper</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">genevre</i> (French <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">genièvre</i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">iūniperus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">juniper</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Hence <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:gin.html>gin</a> rummy</i> (first attested 1941).
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid aaa; font-size: 90%; background: f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><div class="floatnone"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/44px-Wikipedia-logo.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="44" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/66px-Wikipedia-logo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/88px-Wikipedia-logo.png 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200" /></div></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">English Wikipedia <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> an article on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/gin" class="extiw" title="w:gin"><a href = vnd.unilang:gin.html>gin</a></a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/gin" class="extiw" title="w:gin">Wikipedia </a></span></div>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:gin.html>gin</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">gins</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A colourless non-aged alcoholic liquor made by distilling fermented grains such as barley, corn, oats or rye with juniper berries; the base for many <a href = vnd.unilang:cocktails.html>cocktails</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:gin.html>Gin</a> rummy.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">poker</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Drawing the <a href = vnd.unilang:best.html>best</a> card or combination of cards.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:johnny.html>Johnny</a> Chan <a href = vnd.unilang:held.html>held</a> jack-nine, and hit <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gin.html>gin</a></b> when a queen-ten-eight board <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dealt.html>dealt</a> out.</i></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">genever</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">juniper</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Aphetism of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">engin</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">engine</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:gin.html>gin</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">gins</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A trick; a device or instrument.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Contrivance; artifice; a <a href = vnd.unilang:trap.html>trap</a>; a snare.
<dl><dd><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> find and add a quotation of Chaucer to this entry?)</span></dd>
<dd><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> find and add a quotation of Spenser to this entry?)</span></dd></dl></li>
<li>A snare or <a href = vnd.unilang:trap.html>trap</a> for game.</li>
<li>A machine for raising or moving heavy <a href = vnd.unilang:objects.html>objects</a>, consisting of a tripod formed of <a href = vnd.unilang:poles.html>poles</a> united at the top, with a windlass, pulleys, ropes, etc.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mining</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A hoisting drum, usually vertical; a whim.</li>
<li>A pile driver.</li>
<li>A windpump.</li>
<li>A cotton <a href = vnd.unilang:gin.html>gin</a>.</li>
<li>An instrument of torture worked with screws.</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms_2">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">cotton <a href = vnd.unilang:gin.html>gin</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">ginner</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">ginnery</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:gin.html>gin</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">gins</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">ginning</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">ginned</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To remove the seeds from cotton with a cotton <a href = vnd.unilang:gin.html>gin</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To <a href = vnd.unilang:trap.html>trap</a> something in a <a href = vnd.unilang:gin.html>gin</a>.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">ginnen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to begin</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, contraction of <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:beginnen.html>beginnen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">beginnan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*biginnaną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:gin.html>gin</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">gins</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">ginning</b>, <i>simple past</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:gan.html>gan</a></b>, <i>past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">gun</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To begin.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1610–1611</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="w:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>,  “<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Tempest" class="extiw" title="w:The Tempest">The Tempest</a>”, in  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:mr.html>Mr</a>. William Shakespeares Comedies, <a href = vnd.unilang:histories.html>Histories</a>, amp; <a href = vnd.unilang:tragedies.html>Tragedies</a>: Published <a href = vnd.unilang:according.html>According</a> to the True Originall <a href = vnd.unilang:copies.html>Copies</a></cite> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/First_Folio" class="extiw" title="w:First Folio">First Folio</a>), London |  Printed by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Jaggard" class="extiw" title="w:William Jaggard">Isaac Iaggard</a>, and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Edward_Blount" class="extiw" title="w:Edward Blount">Ed[ward] Blount</a>, published 1623, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/606515358">606515358</a></small>, [Act III, scene iii]:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en"><span style="font-variant:small-caps;">Gonzalo</span>: All three of them are deſperate : their great guilt / (Like poyſon giuen to worke a great time after) / Now <b>gins</b> to bite the ſpirits : / <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology 4</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dharug_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dharug language">Dharug</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="xdk">dyin</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">woman</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, but having acquired a derogatory tone.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:gin.html>gin</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">gins</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Australia" class="extiw" title="w:Australia">Australia</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> now considered  offensive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An Aboriginal woman.
<ul><li><b>1869</b>, Thomas Livingstone Mitchell, <i>Three Expeditions into the Interior of Eastern Australia</i>, Volume 1, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://books.google.com.au/books?id=aRQtAAAAYAAJamp;pg=PA273amp;dq=%22gin%22%7C%22gns%22+australia+OR+aboriginal+-intitle:%22%22+-inauthor:%22%22amp;hl=enamp;sa=Xamp;ei=enFdT6a1BcjtmAWIyLnGDwamp;redir_esc=yv=onepageamp;q=%22gin%22%7C%22gns%22%20australia%20OR%20aboriginal%20-intitle%3A%22%22%20-inauthor%3A%22%22amp;f=false">page 273</a>,
<dl><dd>His next shot <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> discharged amongst the mob, and most unfortunately wounded the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gin.html>gin</a></b> already mentioned ; who, with a child fastened to her back, slid down the bank, and lay, apparently dying, with her <a href = vnd.unilang:legs.html>legs</a> in the water.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1894</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:ivan.html>Ivan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dexter.html>Dexter</a>, <i>Talmud: A Strange Narrative of Central Australia</i>, published in serial form in <i>Port Adelaide News and Lefevre's Peninsula Advertiser</i> (SA), Chapter XXI, <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://gutenberg.net.au/ebooks16/1600641.txt">[1]</a>

<li><b>1938</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Xavier_Herbert" class="extiw" title="w:Xavier Herbert">Xavier Herbert</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Capricornia_(novel)" class="extiw" title="w:Capricornia (novel)">Capricornia</a></i>, D. <li><b>2008</b>, Bill Marsh, <a href = vnd.unilang:jack.html>Jack</a> Goldsmith, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:goldie.html>Goldie</a>: Adventures in a <a href = vnd.unilang:vanishing.html>Vanishing</a> Australia</i>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://books.google.com.au/books?id=oIMXK2E80yMCamp;pg=PT66amp;dq=%22gin%22%7C%22gns%22+australia+OR+aboriginal+-intitle:%22%22+-inauthor:%22%22amp;hl=enamp;sa=Xamp;ei=6HddT9uPIenQmAX2xq3PDwamp;redir_esc=yv=onepageamp;q=%22gin%22%7C%22gns%22%20australia%20OR%20aboriginal%20-intitle%3A%22%22%20-inauthor%3A%22%22amp;f=false">unnumbered page</a>,
<dl><dd>But there <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> this <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gin.html>gin</a></b> there, see, what they called a kitchen girl.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ginds.html>ginds</a> (12932)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:ginds.html>ginds</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gins</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:gens.html>gens</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:guns.html>guns</a></i>, akin to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">junt</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">yond</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gothic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gothic language">Gothic</a></span> <i class="Goth mention" lang="got">𐌾𐌰𐌹𐌽𐌳</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="got-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jaind</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. More at <span class="Latn" lang="en">yonder</span>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***gips.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gips.html>gips</a> (13388)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">gypsum</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">γύψος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gúpsos</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, probably from a Semitic language. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gips.html>gips</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>plaster cast</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mineralogy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> gypsum</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
